<script>
(function(){
  var ctx=document.getElementById('distChart').getContext('2d');
  new Chart(ctx,{type:'doughnut',data:{labels:["Close Now", "CX Waiting", "New/No Reply", "Pending", "Review", "IO"],
    datasets:[{data:[878, 127, 0, 46, 92, 151],backgroundColor:["#28a745", "#dc3545", "#fd7e14", "#ffc107", "#0d6efd", "#adb5bd"],borderWidth:2,borderColor:'#fff'}]},
    options:{responsive:true,plugins:{legend:{position:'bottom',labels:{font:{size:11},padding:8}},
    tooltip:{callbacks:{label:function(c){var t=c.dataset.data.reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0);
      return c.label+': '+c.parsed+' ('+Math.round(c.parsed/t*100)+'%)';}}}}
  }});
})();

var dt1;
$(document).ready(function(){
  $('#cxWaitTable').DataTable({pageLength:25,order:[[4,'desc']],
    columnDefs:[{orderable:false,targets:[1,6]}],
    language:{search:'Filter:',lengthMenu:'Show _MENU_'}});
  $('#ghostTable').DataTable({pageLength:25,order:[[4,'desc']],
    language:{search:'Filter:',lengthMenu:'Show _MENU_'}});
  $('#nhTable').DataTable({pageLength:25,order:[[1,'asc']],
    columnDefs:[{orderable:false,targets:[2,5]}],
    language:{search:'Filter:',lengthMenu:'Show _MENU_'}});
  $('#ntTable').DataTable({pageLength:25,order:[[4,'desc']],
    columnDefs:[{orderable:false,targets:[1]}],
    language:{search:'Filter:',lengthMenu:'Show _MENU_'}});

  dt1=$('#ticketTable').DataTable({pageLength:50,order:[],
    columnDefs:[{orderable:false,targets:[1,7]},{width:'80px',targets:4}],
    language:{search:'Search tickets:',lengthMenu:'Show _MENU_ rows'}});

  var agents={};
  $('#ticketBody tr').each(function(){var a=$(this).data('assignee');if(a)agents[a]=true;});
  Object.keys(agents).sort().forEach(function(a){$('#assocFilter').append('<option value="'+a+'">'+a+'</option>');});

  var af='ALL',aa='';
  function applyF(){
    $.fn.dataTable.ext.search=[];
    $.fn.dataTable.ext.search.push(function(s,d,i){
      var row=dt1.row(i).node();
      var p=$(row).data('priority')||'',a=$(row).data('assignee')||'';
      return(af==='ALL'||p===af)&&(!aa||a===aa);
    });dt1.draw();
  }
  $('#filterTabs .tab-btn').on('click',function(){
    $('#filterTabs .tab-btn').removeClass('active');$(this).addClass('active');
    af=$(this).data('filter');applyF();
  });
  $('#assocFilter').on('change',function(){aa=$(this).val();applyF();});
});
</script>
